2/2/22, 15:37 - Yorick Denneman: Alexander of AbonoteichusÂ (Ancient Greek:Â á¼ˆÎ»Î­Î¾Î±Î½Î´ÏÎ¿Ï‚ á½ á¼ˆÎ²Ï‰Î½Î¿Ï„ÎµÎ¹Ï‡Î¯Ï„Î·Ï‚Â AlÃ©xandros ho AbÅnoteichÃ­tÄ“s), also calledÂ Alexander the PaphlagonianÂ (c.â€‰105Â â€“ c.â€‰170Â CE), was aÂ GreekÂ mystic andÂ oracle, and the founder of theÂ GlyconÂ cult that briefly achieved wide popularity in theÂ RomanÂ world. The contemporary writerÂ LucianÂ reports that he was an utter fraud â€“ the god Glycon was supposedly made up of a live snake with an artificial head. The vivid narrative of his career given by Lucian might be taken as fictitious but for the corroboration of certain coins of the emperorsÂ Lucius VerusÂ andÂ Marcus Aurelius and of a statue of Alexander, said byÂ AthenagorasÂ to have stood in the forum ofÂ Parium.Â There is further evidence from inscriptions.

At least initially, the cult did not worship an abstraction or a spirit of a snake but an actual, physical serpent that was said to embody the god. According to the cult's mythology, the snake appeared after Alexander had foretold the coming of a new incarnation ofÂ Asclepius. When the people gathered in the marketplace of Abonutichus at noon, when the incarnation was supposed to occur, Alexander produced a goose egg and sliced it open, revealing the god within. Within a week it grew to the size of a man with the features of a man on its face, including long blond hair. At this point the figure resembling this description was apparently a puppet that appeared in the temple. In some references Glycon was a trained snake with a puppet head.
As with previous Macedonian snake cults, the focus of worship at the temple was on fertility. Barren women would bring offerings to Glycon in hopes of becoming pregnant. According to Lucian, Alexander had less magical ways of causing pregnancy among his flock as well.

By 160, the worship of Glycon had undoubtedly spread beyond the Aegean. An inscription fromÂ AntiochÂ of that date records a slogan, "Glycon protect us from the plague-cloud" that is consistent with the description we have from Lucian. Also in that year theÂ governorÂ of Asia,Â Publius Mummius Sisenna Rutilianus, declared himself protector of Glycon's oracle. The governor later married Alexander's daughter. According to Lucian, another Roman governor, ofÂ Cappadocia, was led by Glycon's oracle to his death inÂ Armenia, and even the Emperor himself was not immune to the cult:Â Marcus AureliusÂ sought prophesies from Alexander and his snake god.

Meanwhile,Â Abonoteichos, a small fishing village before the arrival of the cult, became an important town and accepted another name,Â Ionopolis. It is uncertain what role the popularity of Glycon played in the rise of the city.
As the cult had an established popularity with the lower social strataÂ and later several important Roman functionaries and officials were counted among the believers in Glycon and the prophecies of Alexander,Â including the Emperor at the time, Marcus Aurelius.Â Such endorsement by the ruling classes coupled with pre existing superstitions of serpents as possessing healing powers, the cult of Glycon likely found no shortage of converts and adherents in new areas of the Roman world.

6/22/22, 21:28 - Terry Vreeburg: Beste Groene Hand,

Gefeliciteerd, vandaag is het Wereld Groene Hand Dag! 

Sterker nog, vanaf vandaag is het elk jaar op 22 juni Wereld Groene Hand dag. 

Wellicht zullen jullie je het nog wel herinneren dat zo een (kleine?) twintig jaar geleden, vermoedelijk in het Melkwout, het idee tot stand kwam om op 22 juni van het jaar 2022 samen te komen op ons stekkie op het Wed.

Om te zien wat dan onze status is als mens maar vooral als Groene Hand.

Dat idee kwam wellicht gelijk op, samen met het ontluiken van een besef van stervelijkheid alsmede de smaak van nostalgie die hoort bij de capriolen van de adolecentie.

Welnu, het moment is daar.

Van een samenkomen is het er duidelijk niet van gekomen, niet om het minste omdat men tegenwoordig in het buitenland woont, of dat ambieert.

Maar goed, ik ben toch maar even naar het Wed gegaan om een duik te nemen en namens jullie allen dit moment te vieren.

Zonder bier en zonder joint. En ook niet op onze stek, want daar zitten nu een nieuwe generatie lozers.

Toch leuk dat 'we' nog bestaan!

Tot volgend jaar!

Uw Groene Hand lid, afdeling Schalkwijk.
